Electronic Text of the Atharvavedaparisistas

Based on the edition by George Melville Bolling and Julius von Negelein:
"The ParishiShTtas of the Atharvaveda",
Vol. 1, parts 1 and 2 (all published), Leipzig: Harrassowitz 1909-1910

Input by Yuri Ishii (Tokai University)
Revised by Arlo Griffiths (Leiden and Groningen Universities)
in collaboration with Reinhold Gruenendahl (Niedersaechsische Staats- und Universitaetsbibliothek, Goettingen)


ANALYTIC VESION (BHELA conventions)

ANALYTIC VERSION according to BHELA conventions:

Sandhi markers:
(. =short vowel, - =long vowel)

in word-sandhi:
1: . .  e.g.: veda+anta = vedA1nta
2: - .
3: . -
4: - -
 
in sentence-sandhi:
7: . .  e.g.: ca+api = cA7pi
8: . -
9: - .
0: - -

(ParishiShTa_51. grahayuddham)
(AVParis_51,1.1)	oM ke cid grahA nArarAn Ashrayante ke cid grahA [jyotiShi] saMgrahe ca/ graho graheNai7va hataH kathaM syAd vij~nAya tattvaM bhagavAn bravItu  ||
